***significant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:significant.html>significant</a> (788)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology"><a href = vnd.unilang:etymology.html>Etymology</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">significans</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">significare</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">signum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:sign.html>sign</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ficare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:do.html>do</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:make.html>make</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:significant.html>significant</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:comparative.html>comparative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:significant.html>significant</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:superlative.html>superlative</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:most.html>most</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:significant.html>significant</a></b>)
